######### printf_lover_v2 ##########
######### printf-tester ##########
######### ft_printf_test ##########
- [OUTPUT] ft_printf("%5%")
   expected: "    %"
   actual:   ""

- [OUTPUT] ft_printf("%-5%")
   expected: "%    "
   actual:   ""

- [OUTPUT] ft_printf("%05%")
   expected: "0000%"
   actual:   ""

- [OUTPUT] ft_printf("%-05%")
   expected: "%    "
   actual:   ""

- [OUTPUT] ft_printf("%.p", &ncm_p)
   expected: "0x10d3c50d0"
   actual:   "0xd3c50d0"

- [OUTPUT] ft_printf("%-p", &ncm_p)
   expected: "0x10d3c50d0"
   actual:   "0xd3c50d0"

- [OUTPUT] ft_printf("%-s", NULL)
   expected: "(null)"
   actual:   ""

- [OUTPUT] ft_printf("%23s", NULL)
   expected: "                 (null)"
   actual:   ""

- [OUTPUT] ft_printf("%s", NULL)
   expected: "(null)"
   actual:   ""

- [OUTPUT] ft_printf("%32s", "abc")
   expected: "                             abc"
   actual:   "abc"

- [OUTPUT] ft_printf("%16s", "nark nark")
   expected: "       nark nark"
   actual:   "nark nark"

- [OUTPUT] ft_printf("%-32s", "abc")
   expected: "abc                             "
   actual:   "abc"

- [OUTPUT] ft_printf("%-16s", "nark nark")
   expected: "nark nark       "
   actual:   "nark nark"

- [OUTPUT] ft_printf("%.5s%7s", "yo", "boi")
   expected: "yo    boi"
   actual:   "yoboi"

- [OUTPUT] ft_printf("%7.5s", "yolo")
   expected: "   yolo"
   actual:   "yolo"

- [OUTPUT] ft_printf("%7.5s", "bombastic")
   expected: "  bomba"
   actual:   "bomba"

- [OUTPUT] ft_printf("%-7.5s", "yolo")
   expected: "yolo   "
   actual:   "yolo"

- [OUTPUT] ft_printf("%-7.5s", "tubular")
   expected: "tubul  "
   actual:   "tubul"

- [OUTPUT] ft_printf("%7.7s%7.7s", "hello", "world")
   expected: "  hello  world"
   actual:   "helloworld"

- [OUTPUT] ft_printf("%3.7s%7.7s", "hello", "world")
   expected: "hello  world"
   actual:   "helloworld"

- [OUTPUT] ft_printf("%7.7s%3.7s", "hello", "world")
   expected: "  helloworld"
   actual:   "helloworld"

- [OUTPUT] ft_printf("%7.3s%7.7s", "hello", "world")
   expected: "    hel  world"
   actual:   "helworld"

- [OUTPUT] ft_printf("%3.3s%7.7s", "hello", "world")
   expected: "hel  world"
   actual:   "helworld"

- [OUTPUT] ft_printf("%7.3s%3.7s", "hello", "world")
   expected: "    helworld"
   actual:   "helworld"

- [OUTPUT] ft_printf("%7.7s%7.3s", "hello", "world")
   expected: "  hello    wor"
   actual:   "hellowor"

- [OUTPUT] ft_printf("%3.7s%7.3s", "hello", "world")
   expected: "hello    wor"
   actual:   "hellowor"

- [OUTPUT] ft_printf("%7.7s%3.3s", "hello", "world")
   expected: "  hellowor"
   actual:   "hellowor"

- [OUTPUT] ft_printf("%7.3s%7.3s", "hello", "world")
   expected: "    hel    wor"
   actual:   "helwor"

- [OUTPUT] ft_printf("%3.3s%7.3s", "hello", "world")
   expected: "hel    wor"
   actual:   "helwor"

- [OUTPUT] ft_printf("%7.3s%3.3s", "hello", "world")
   expected: "    helwor"
   actual:   "helwor"
